              ETK Kablo, whichs main principle is quality, is founded in 1979 in Istanbul, T√ºrkiye to manufacture telephone cables. ETK Kablo became a global leading manufacturer and exporter of low current and fiber optic cables within years, correctly applied the reshaped needs with its completely computer aided machinery, expert and experienced personnel abiding to the international standards and norms.
	In the year 2001, ETK Kablo built its fiber optic cable manufacturing facility to adjust the changing and evolving technology and now ETK Kablo has one of the highest capacity on fiber optic cables. In its current fiber optic cable manufacturing facility, it is capable of manufacturing fiber optic cables up to 432 optical fiber cores, various single mode and various multi-mode, mini, microduct, armored, multi armored, non-metallic armored, single loose tubed, multi loose tubed, tight buffered, hybrid, composite, flame retardant, fire resistant, single jacketed, multi jacketed, messenger wired, all-dielectric self-supporting (ADSS), other various types according to the customer specifications.
	ETK Kablo has a global and respectable place, with the principles of correct product, correct time and correct price, just in time delivery, perfectness, minimum waste, strong pre-sales and after-sales activities, continuous improvement, environmentally-conscious, respectful to the employee rights, utmost occupational safety in its presence in more than 120 countries of 5 continents with the principle of quality first on all of its products and services.

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">üí™ Steel Strength, Fiber Speed: ETK Kablo‚Äôs Steel Wire Armored Fiber Optic Cables
¬†
At ETK Kablo, we take pride in delivering fiber optic solutions that combine maximum protection with uncompromised performance.
¬†
Our Steel Wire Armored (SWA) Fiber Optic Cables are engineered for the most demanding environments, ensuring:

 ‚úÖ Superior mechanical protection against impact and rodent attacks
 ‚úÖ Reliable performance in harsh outdoor conditions
 ‚úÖ High tensile strength for direct burial and industrial applications
 ‚úÖ Wide fiber options (Singlemode G.652D, G.657A1/A2 and Multimode  OM1‚ÄìOM5)
 ‚úÖ Compliance with international standards for long-term durability
¬†
With exports to more than 120 countries across 5 continents, ETK Kablo stands as a trusted global manufacturer ‚Äî proudly representing T√ºrkiye in the world of advanced cabling.

Whether for telecom networks, data centers, or critical infrastructure projects, our armored fiber optic cables provide the resilience and stability your networks demand.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Building More Capacity With Less Cable ‚ö°

ETK Kablo‚Äôs flex-module fiber optic cables pair G.657.A2 bend-insensitive fibers with kink-resistant mini-modules to protect performance in tight pathways.

The result ‚Üí high fiber density for better duct utilization and lower civil works, plus a lighter, more manageable cable for faster pulls.

Key Advantages:

 ‚úÖ Bend-insensitive performance: stable attenuation in confined routes
 ‚úÖ Kink-resistant modules: helps avoid micro-bends and signal loss
 ‚úÖ High-density architecture: more fibers per duct, smaller outer diameters
 ‚úÖ Easy handling: smaller, lighter, more flexible construction
 ‚úÖ Tool-free access: modules open cleanly for rapid fiber prep

ETK Kablo manufactures to international standards and tailors designs to your project‚Äôs route, duct, and CPR requirements. üåç

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">üî• Myth vs. Fact üî•

‚ùå Myth: ‚ÄúAll cables stop working during a fire.‚Äù

‚úÖ Fact: Fire-resistant cables, like ETK‚Äôs FE180 / PH120 designs, are engineered to maintain circuit integrity even under extreme fire conditions. These cables ensure that emergency lighting, alarms, and critical communication systems continue to operate when they are needed most.

While standard cables can fail within minutes of exposure to flames, fire-resistant cables are tested to withstand fire for up to 180 minutes‚Äîproviding life-saving reliability in hospitals, airports, tunnels, and high-rise buildings. 

At ETK Kablo, we don‚Äôt just design cables to connect the world‚Äîwe design them to protect it. üåç
